STAT table

STAT table

Info

Frank Ruhl Libre Light Regular (FrankRuhlLibre-Light.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

Info

Frank Ruhl Libre Regular (FrankRuhlLibre-Regular.ttf)

STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

No check of STAT table for static fonts included, yet. Static fonts do not need to have a STAT table. It is only recommended by Microsoft, not required.
More infos here:
https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/typography/opentype/spec/stat

Frank Ruhl Libre Light Regular (FrankRuhlLibre-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Frank Ruhl Libre' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Frank Ruhl Libre Light'.

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'FrankRuhlLibre-Regular', Everything looks good.

Pass

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'FrankRuhlLibre-Medium', Everything looks good.

Frank Ruhl Libre Medium Regular (FrankRuhlLibre-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Frank Ruhl Libre' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Frank Ruhl Libre Medium'.

Pass

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Frank Ruhl Libre' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Black' = NID 1 'Frank Ruhl Libre Black'.

Every PostScript name is fine.

sinf

If there is a feature subs, then the sinf feature should be there, too. Otherwise InDesign will mark it not existing.

There is a subs feature in the font, but the sinf is missing. Please investigate.
